BUSINESS General Walmart Inc. `` Walmart `` Company `` helps people around world save money live better – anytime anywhere – retail stores eCommerce Through innovation striving create customer-centric experience seamlessly integrates eCommerce retail stores omnichannel offering saves time customers Each week serve nearly 270 million customers visit 11,700 stores numerous eCommerce websites 65 banners 28 countries Our strategy lead price invest differentiate access competitive assortment deliver great experience Leading price designed earn trust customers every day providing broad assortment quality merchandise services everyday low prices `` EDLP EDLP pricing philosophy price items low price every day customers trust prices change frequent promotional activity Price leadership core Everyday low cost `` EDLC commitment control expenses cost savings passed along customers Our omni-channel presence provides customers access broad assortment anytime anywhere We strive give customers members great digital physical shopping experience Our operations comprise three reportable segments Walmart U.S. Walmart International Sam 's Club Our fiscal year ends January 31 United States `` U.S. Canadian operations We consolidate operations generally using one-month lag calendar year basis Our discussion fiscal years ended January 31 2018 `` fiscal 2018 `` January 31 2017 `` fiscal 2017 `` January 31 2016 `` fiscal 2016 `` During fiscal 2018 generated total revenues 500.3 billion primarily comprised net sales 495.8 billion We maintain principal offices 702 S.W 8th Street Bentonville Arkansas 72716 USA Our common stock trades New York Stock Exchange symbol `` WMT The Development Our Company Although Walmart incorporated Delaware October 1969 businesses conducted founders began 1945 Sam M. Walton opened franchise Ben Franklin variety store Newport Arkansas In 1946 brother James L. Walton opened similar store Versailles Missouri Until 1962 founders ' business devoted entirely operation variety stores In year first Wal-Mart Discount City discount store opened Rogers Arkansas In 1983 opened first Sam 's Club 1988 opened first supercenter In 1998 opened first Neighborhood Market In 1991 began first international initiative entered joint venture Mexico Since international presence expanded January 31 2018 Walmart International segment conducted business 27 countries In 2000 began first eCommerce initiative creating walmart.com That year also created samsclub.com Since digital presence continued grow In 2007 walmart.com launched Site Store service enabling customers make purchase online pick merchandise stores In 2016 acquired jet.com U.S. formed strategic alliance JD.com China Subsequent jet.com purchase acquired several U.S. eCommerce entities In 2017 walmart.com launched free two-day shipping 2 million items created Store N 8 tech incubator focus drive commerce forward These eCommerce efforts led omni-channel offerings many markets including 1,100 `` Online Grocery pickup locations U.S. Information About Our Segments The Company engaged operation retail wholesale units well eCommerce websites located throughout U.S. Africa Argentina Brazil Canada Central America Chile China India Japan Mexico United Kingdom The Company 's operations conducted three reportable segments Walmart U.S. Walmart International Sam 's Club The Company defines segments operations whose results chief operating decision maker `` CODM regularly reviews analyze performance allocate resources The Company sells similar individual products services segments It impractical segregate identify revenues individual products services Walmart U.S. largest segment operates retail stores 50 states U.S. Washington D.C.
